一刀流〝切落〟は敵の一撃に対して全く対称の一撃をもって迎え、これを切り落とし、更に敵の肉体をも断つ技法。
Ito-ryu "cutting off" is a technique that greets the enemy with a completely symmetrical blow, cuts it off, and cuts off the enemy's body.

双方が同等の企図をもって打ち合った場合、剣撃の威力と精密さで上回った側が勝利を収める。　今の一合は俺が優越した。

The meeting and crossing Sorimachi ran up to the sky as it was-it keeps rising. If you follow the rules of the cavalry battle, you have to go around the helmet angle and move down to gain speed in preparation for the next match.

ならば高度優勢を奪取するための奇手――まさか。　このような方法で上位を取ったところで意味はない。時間が掛かり過ぎる。高度を得、反転、突撃に入ろうとした時には、全てを終えた敵を目前に迎えるだろう。

Then, aiming for the chance that this descended, attack from the sky. --There is this. That man would use that kind of skill without any effort.

（乗らぬ）

Follow the rising shadow of Sorimachi. No effort is required to close the gap. Enemy horses that continue to oppose gravity are no longer significantly slower.

それでいながら、尚も昇ってゆく。　あまつさえ、兜角を更に引き上げて。

速力という空の戦いにあっては得難い代価を湯尽し、竜騎兵は高度を貪る。　際限なく。止め処なく。飽き足らず。
The dragoons devour altitude, exhausting the price that is difficult to obtain in the sky battle of speed. Endlessly. Without stopping. Not tired.

What does Sorimachi think? Is it just because of the badness of giving up that the policy is not changed after being tracked?

当方とて速度はみるみる減殺されている。　だが勢力を充分に確保してのち上昇に転じた村正と、太刀打からそのまま上昇に移った竜騎兵との差は厳然。詰まってはいるものの、優劣は明確に有る。
For me, the speed has been diminished. However, the difference between Muramasa, who secured enough power and then started to rise, and the dragoons, who moved from sword fighting to rising, is severe. Although it is clogged, there are clear advantages and disadvantages.

打ち間に捕捉するのは時間の問題。　雪車町が迎撃に転じたとしても、態勢を整える前に斬り伏せられる。
It's only a matter of time before you catch it in between. Even if Sorimachi turns to interception, it will be cut down before it is ready.

王手を掛けられている事に、彼は気付いている筈だ。　然りながら翔天を止めない。

月の狂気に魅入られ、戦いを忘れたのか――　そんな事さえ思う。
Did you forget the fight because you were fascinated by the madness of the moon? I even think about that.

戦慄すべきはその低速域制御力だった。　通常であれば失速していてもおかしくない――いや失速しているべき危険域まで速度を落としながら、彼の見えない手綱は騎体をなお完璧に御している。
What was terrifying was its low-speed control. It's okay to stall normally-no, slowing down to the danger zone where he should be stalling, his invisible reins still perfectly control the horse.

精強さでは人後に落ちない六波羅の正規兵であっても、この域では揚力を手放し、錐揉みして落ちてゆくほかに術を持たないだろう。　百万騎を号す六波羅、その幾人がこの男に倣えるか。
Even Rokuhara's regular soldiers, who do not fall behind in terms of strength, will have no choice but to let go of lift and rub them down in this area. Rokuhara, who issues a million horses, how many of them can imitate this man?

九〇式竜騎兵甲の性能とは到底思われない。　雪車町一蔵の性能に他ならなかった。
I can't think of the performance of the 90-type dragoon instep. It was none other than the performance of Sorimachi Ichizo.

後尾に迫る。　こちらの速力も既に危険域だった。わずかでも気を抜けばその刹那、俺は空から地上へ蹴り落とされるだろう。
Approaching the tail. This speed was already in the danger zone. If you take a little care, that moment, I will be kicked from the sky to the ground.

間違ってもそんな無様は晒せない。　速度の差はここに至って零に近くなりつつあるも、しかしまだ確在。敵騎はより苛酷な騎航を成し遂げているというに、こちらが先に屈せようか。
Even if you make a mistake, you cannot expose such a mischief. The speed difference is getting closer to zero, but it's still there. Enemy horses have achieved more severe voyages, but should we succumb first?

あと一歩。　あと一歩で斬れる。
One more step. You can cut it in one step.

彼我二騎の描く軌道はもはや垂直上昇に近い。　このような騎航は何秒も保たない。
The trajectory drawn by him is almost vertical. Such a ride does not last for seconds.

There is no inferiority in Sorimachi now. Good posture.

The speed ratio-reverses. Because pure gravity-vertical gravity adds to Sorimachi.

垂直方向の重力。　俺が今、真っ向から敵にしているもの。
Gravity in the vertical direction. What I'm heading for right now.

寸毫の間に始まりそして終わった、完璧な逆転劇。　観客の心境で、既に益体もない知識を引き出す。
A perfect reversal drama that started and ended in the middle of a háo. In the mind of the audience, draw out knowledge that is already unprofitable.

…………あれは。　一刀流の始祖・伊東一刀斎が、師である中条流鐘巻自斎から受け継いだ五つの秘法――
…………That is. Five secret methods inherited from the founder of Ito-ryu, Ito Itosai, from his teacher, Chujo-ryu Kanemaki Jisai.

一刀流の最極意。　妙剣／絶妙剣／真剣／独妙剣……
The ultimate in one-sword style. Mysterious sword / Exquisite sword / Serious / Original sword ……

そして。　この――――
And. this----

〝金翅鳥王剣〟
"Kingu Toriou Sword"

マックス・インメルマン中尉。　外暦一九一四年から一九一八年にわたって戦われた欧州戦争において、比類なき勇名を鳴り響かせた独逸の誇る撃墜王の一人である。
Lieutenant Max Immelmann. He is one of the proud shooting down kings who made an unparalleled heroic name in the European War, which was fought from 1914 to 1918.

その名に〝侯〟の一語が無い事からも明らかな通り、彼は竜騎兵団に属してはいたものの、騎士階級の出身ではなかった。　真打劔冑の継承者ではなかったのである。
As is clear from the lack of the word "Hou" in his name, he belonged to the Dragoons, but was not from the knighthood. He was not the successor to the Shinto Kabuto.

この時代の撃墜王としては異例と云わねばならない。　外暦一九〇〇年代初頭（国紀二五〇〇年代中盤）はまだ数打劔冑が開発されて間もない頃であり、現在に比べれば性能は著しく低いレベルに留まっていた。
It must be said that it is unusual for a shooting down king of this era. In the early 1900s of the foreign calendar (mid-250s of the national era), a few helmets had just been developed, and their performance remained at a significantly lower level than they are today.

彼が愛騎としたフォッカーＥ３とてもそうだ。　張線支持を採用した単翼騎――当時代の技術の粋が凝らされた騎体ではあったが、真打劔冑との性能差を埋めるものでは到底ない。
The Fokker E3 he loved is so. Single-winged horse with support for stretched wire-Although it was a horse body with elaborate technology of the present era, it cannot fill the performance difference with the true helmet.

その頃、戦場に華を添えた各国の撃墜王――由緒正しい名門の騎士であり最高の劔冑を継承していた人々――と、一介の騎兵将校インメルマンとの間に、騎体性能の点で巨大な隔絶があったことは確実である。
At that time, the point of horse body performance between the shooting down kings of each country who added glamor to the battlefield-people who were venerable prestigious knights and inherited the best helmet-and one cavalry officer Immelman. It is certain that there was a huge isolation.

しかも、彼の配属された北フランス戦線は敵に正規の騎士が多く、対して味方の騎士は大半が対露戦線に派遣されていたためほとんど皆無という、実に苛酷を極める状況下にあった。
Moreover, the North France front to which he was assigned had many regular knights as enemies, while most of his knights were dispatched to the Russian front, so there were almost no knights, and the situation was extremely harsh.

味方は彼を含めて新弱の竜騎兵ばかり。　敵方は古強の騎士が居並ぶ。　……武功を掲げるどころか、生き残るだけでも至難であったに違いない。
Allies, including him, are all new dragoons. The enemy is lined with old-fashioned knights. It must have been extremely difficult just to survive, rather than to raise martial arts.

その死線にあってインメルマンを撃墜王たらしめたのは、少年期に出会った異国人との体験だった。
It was an experience with a foreigner I met in my childhood that made Immelman the king who shot down at that deadline.

徳川時代の幕引き後、大和はやや閉鎖的であった前時代の反動のように西洋文化を多く取り入れ、何それとなく学んだが、軍事編制においてはプロイセン――ドイツに倣う所が非常に多かった。
After the curtain of the Tokugawa era, Yamato took in a lot of Western culture and learned somehow like the reaction of the previous era, which was a little closed, but in military organization there were many places that imitated Prussia-Germany.

プロイセン軍こそ欧州最精強と見る向きが強かったためである。　幾度となく軍事交流団が派遣され、貪欲に技術知識を求めた。
This is because the Prussian army was strongly regarded as the strongest in Europe. Military exchange teams were dispatched many times and greedily sought technical knowledge.

そうして、ドイツに渡った男の一人に……
Then, to one of the men who went to Germany ...

小野派一刀流一六代宗家、笹木純蔵がいたのだ。
There was Junzo Sasaki, the 16th Soke of the Ono school Ichiroku style.

彼はふとした事から知り合ったインメルマン少年に、一刀流剣術を手解きし、その才の尋常ならざるを知るや、奥義の伝授まで行った。……軽々しいというか、気前が良いというか、いささか変人だったようである。
He learned the Ito-ryu swordsmanship to the Immelman boy he met by accident, and when he learned that his talent was extraordinary, he even taught the mystery. ...... It seems that he was a little weird, light or generous.

だが彼は帰国の後、国粋の文化を売ったとしてこの行為に批判を浴びると、こう応えて一蹴した。　――学ぶのみで教えぬ者は、即ち知恵の盗人である。自分はドイツ軍に学び、返礼として少年に教えたのだ。
However, after returning to Japan, he was criticized for selling the national culture and dismissed it in response. --A person who only learns and does not teach is a thief of wisdom. I learned from the German army and taught the boy in return.

かくしてインメルマンは一刀流の秘奥を拝受したのだが、教えた笹木にして彼がその秘技を活用できるだろうとまでは考えていなかったに違いない。
Thus, Immelman received the secret of the one-sword style, but he must not have thought that he could utilize the secret technique with Sasaki who taught him.

一刀流五箇の秘伝は絶えず伝えられてきてこそいたものの、余りの難解さに使い得た者は始祖以来ついになく、技術ではなく単なる知識になり果てていた。　免許皆伝を示す一種の形式に過ぎなかったのである。
Although the secrets of the five Ito-ryu styles have been constantly passed down, no one has been able to use them for too much difficulty since their ancestors, and they have become mere knowledge rather than technology. It was just a kind of form showing all licenses.

だが、北仏戦線の極限状況にあって――　敵の剛強な騎士に追われたマックス・インメルマンは、差し迫る死に抗う渦中で遂に、秘剣の一つを蘇生させるに至ったのだ。
However, in the extreme situation of the Northern French Front-after being chased by a mighty enemy knight, Max Immelmann finally revived one of his secret swords in a whirlpool of imminent death.

金翅鳥王剣。　垂直騎航からの反転落下攻撃。　自己より圧倒的に優る敵を討つ、起死回生の剣。
Golden winged bird king sword. Reverse fall attack from vertical cavalry. A sword of rebirth that defeats enemies that are overwhelmingly superior to oneself.

以後、インメルマンは常にこの技と共にあり、幾多の騎士を空から墜として敵味方を瞠目させた。　彼と彼の技は同一視され、その名は欧州を席巻し、悪魔的な恐怖と戦神的な畏怖の的となった。
Since then, Immelman has always been with this technique, dropping many knights from the sky and staring at his enemies and allies. He and his skill were equated, and the name swept Europe and became the target of demonic horror and war-god awe.

一九一六年に戦死するまで、生涯の撃墜数は一七騎。　全てがフランスの名だたる騎士である。
Until he died in 1916, he shot down 17 horses in his lifetime. All are famous knights of France.

現在なおその名は語り継がれ、知らぬ者とていない。　最強、無敵、魔剣、神技――彼の死と共に消え失せた、戦場の幻影を示すものとして、諸国の軍人そして歴史書はその名をいつまでも叫び続ける。
Even now, the name has been handed down, and he is not a stranger. The strongest, invincible, magic sword, divine technique-military personnel and history books of the nations continue to scream their name as an indication of the illusion of the battlefield that disappeared with his death.

〝インメルマンの反転〟と。
With "Reversal of Immelman".

《みど……っ……いる?　きっ……ぃを………ない………》
《Mido ……………… Are you there?

村正の声が遠い。　視界は昏い――朱い。
Muramasa's voice is far away. The field of vision is dull-vermilion.

どれほどの損傷を受けたのか。　他人事のようにはたらく意識が、現状から類推した。
How much damage did you get? The consciousness of working like other personnel was inferred from the current situation.

瀕死。
dying.
